```mermaid
flowchart TD
    A[Start main] --> B[Parse command line arguments]
    B --> C[Initialize SparkContext with YARN]
    C --> D[Configure Spark settings]
    D --> E[Get max_id from PostgreSQL]
    E --> F{Successfully got max_id?}
    F -->|No| G[Set max_id = 6000000000]
    F -->|Yes| H[Load table from PostgreSQL]
    G --> H
    H --> I[Try to load latest_df from S3]
    I --> J{latest_df loaded?}
    J -->|Yes| K[Get max_id from latest_df]
    K --> L[Filter df where id > max_id]
    L --> M[Write df to versioned S3 path]
    M --> N[Re-read df from S3]
    N --> O[Add JSON columns from value field]
    O --> P[Cast date columns to TimestampType]
    P --> Q[Append to latest S3 path]
    Q --> R[End]
    J -->|No| S[Write df to versioned S3 path]
    S --> T[Write df to latest S3 path]
    T --> R
```

path</p></span></div></foreignObject></g></g></g></g></g></svg>

## Diagram 3

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
    participant Script
    participant PostgreSQL
    participant S3
    participant Spark
    
    Script->>Spark: Initialize SparkContext
    Script->>PostgreSQL: Query max(id) from table
    PostgreSQL-->>Script: Return max_id
    Script->>PostgreSQL: Load table with partitioning
    PostgreSQL-->>Spark: Return DataFrame
    Script->>S3: Try read latest parquet
    alt Latest data exists
        S3-->>Spark: Return latest_df
        Script->>Spark: Filter new records (id > max_id)
        Script->>S3: Write to versioned path
        Script->>S3: Read back from versioned path
        Script->>Spark: Transform and add JSON columns
        Script->>S3: Append to latest path
    else No latest data
        Script->>S3: Write to versioned path
        Script->>S3: Write to latest path
    end
```

## Diagram 4

```mermaid
classDiagram
    class main {
        +table: str
        +DB_HOSTNAME: str
        +DB_PORT: int
        +DB_USERNAME: str
        +DB_PASSWORD: str
        +DATABASE: str
        +s3_output_path: str
        +read_postgresql()
        +load_latest_s3()
        +filter_incremental()
        +transform_json_columns()
        +write_to_s3()
    }
    class SparkContext {
        +master: str
        +_conf: SparkConf
        +set_network_timeout()
        +set_heartbeat_interval()
    }
    class SQLContext {
        +read: DataFrameReader
        +sql()
    }
    class DataFrame {
        +filter()
        +withColumn()
        +write: DataFrameWriter
        +agg()
        +collect()
    }
    main --> SparkContext
    main --> SQLContext
    SQLContext --> DataFrame
    SparkContext --> SQLContext
```

## Diagram 5

```mermaid
stateDiagram-v2
    [*] --> Initialize
    Initialize --> QueryMaxId: Setup Spark
    QueryMaxId --> LoadTable: Get max_id
    LoadTable --> CheckLatest: Load from PostgreSQL
    CheckLatest --> IncrementalMode: latest_df exists
    CheckLatest --> FullMode: No latest_df
    IncrementalMode --> FilterRecords: Found existing data
    FilterRecords --> WriteVersioned: Filter id > max_id
    WriteVersioned --> TransformData: Write to S3
    TransformData --> AppendLatest: Add JSON columns
    AppendLatest --> [*]: Complete
    FullMode --> WriteVersioned2: First run
    WriteVersioned2 --> WriteLatest: Write versioned
    WriteLatest --> [*]: Complete
```
